# LoCoBench-Agent Task

## Overview

**Task ID**: c_ml_nlp_expert_017_architectural_understanding_expert_01
**Category**: architectural_understanding
**Difficulty**: expert
**Language**: c
**Context Length**: 946983 tokens
**Files**: 77

## Task Title

Analysis and Critique of the MVC Pattern in the LexiLearn C-based ML Orchestrator

## Description

The LexiLearn Orchestrator is a complex, C-based system for managing NLP model pipelines, featuring automated retraining, monitoring, and versioning. The system's architecture is unconventionally based on the Model-View-Controller (MVC) pattern, a design choice more common in user-facing applications. A deep understanding of this architectural decision and its implementation is critical for maintaining and extending the system. This task requires the agent to deconstruct this architecture, map its components to the MVC roles, trace a critical data flow through the system, and provide a reasoned critique of the pattern's suitability for this domain.

## Your Task

You are a senior software architect tasked with onboarding a new team member. To do this, you need to create a definitive guide to the LexiLearn Orchestrator's architecture. Your primary focus is to explain the system's core MVC design pattern and its implications.

Perform the following actions:

1.  **Map Components to MVC Roles:** Based on the provided source code, identify which high-level directories and key components (e.g., `orchestrator.c`, `pipeline_manager.h`, `model_registry.c`, `dashboard_server.c`, `model_monitor.h`) map to the Model, the View, and the Controller. Justify your mapping.

2.  **Describe Communication Pathways:** Explain the primary communication mechanisms and data flow between the Model, View, and Controller layers. How does the Controller command the Model? How does the Model report state changes? How is the View updated with new information from the other layers?

3.  **Trace a Critical Workflow:** Trace the complete sequence of events and component interactions that occur when the `DriftDetector` (`src/controller/monitoring/drift_detector.h`) identifies a significant data drift, which in turn triggers an automated retraining job. Detail the path of this event, starting from the detector and following it through the relevant controller, pipeline, and scheduler components until a new training job is ready to run.

4.  **Critique the Architecture:** Provide a critical analysis of using the MVC pattern for this C-based ML orchestration system. What are the primary benefits this pattern provides in this context? What are the most significant drawbacks or architectural smells that arise from this choice? Be specific and reference the project's domain (ML orchestration) and implementation language (C).

## Expected Approach

An expert developer would approach this by first forming a high-level hypothesis based on the directory structure (`src/model`, `src/view`, `src/controller`) and the `docs/architecture.md` file. They would then dive into the code to verify and refine this understanding.

1.  **Mapping:** The developer would analyze the header files in each directory. They'd identify that `src/model` contains all ML-related logic (data, pipelines, models, feature store), `src/view` contains the `dashboard_server` for reporting, and `src/controller` contains the orchestration logic, schedulers, and monitors that tie everything together. `orchestrator.c` would be identified as the central controller.

2.  **Communication:** They would look for patterns of interaction. They'd see that the Controller (`orchestrator.c`, `pipeline_manager.c`) makes direct function calls to the Model components (`model_trainer.c`, `feature_store_manager.c`) to initiate actions. For feedback, they would identify the use of an observer pattern (`observer.h`) where Model-related components (like `model_monitor.c`) can notify the Controller of events (like drift detection) without being tightly coupled. The Controller would then update the View (`dashboard_server.c`) by pushing log data or status updates.

3.  **Tracing:** This requires careful file-hopping. The developer would trace the 'retraining' signal:
    - Start at `drift_detector.h/.c` to see how drift is detected and signaled.
    - Move to its user, `model_monitor.h/.c`, which aggregates monitoring events.
    - Find where `model_monitor` reports its findings. This likely involves the `observer.h` pattern, notifying the main `orchestrator.c`.
    - The `orchestrator.c` would then consult the `retraining_trigger.h/.c` component to decide if a retraining is warranted.
    - Upon confirmation, the `orchestrator.c` would call the `pipeline_manager.h/.c` to construct a new training pipeline.
    - The `pipeline_manager.c` would use the `job_factory.c` to create a training job.
    - Finally, this job would be handed off to the `task_scheduler.h/.c` for execution.

4.  **Critique:** The developer would synthesize their findings into a balanced critique:
    - **Benefits:** Good separation of concerns (ML logic is separate from orchestration and reporting), modularity (easy to add a new model to `src/model` or a new view to `src/view`), and provides a clear, high-level structure to a complex system.
    - **Drawbacks:** MVC is designed for user interaction loops, not long-running, event-driven backend processes. This can lead to a bloated 'Controller' layer that manages too much state and logic. The communication between the 'Model' (e.g., a training pipeline) and 'Controller' can be inefficient or awkward in C, potentially relying on complex callbacks or polling, unlike the clean data binding in typical MVC frameworks. The 'View' is also non-standard, being a data server rather than a GUI, which stretches the metaphor.

## Evaluation Criteria

- **Component Mapping Accuracy:** Did the agent correctly map the key directories and files to their MVC roles?
- **Communication Pathway Identification:** Did the agent correctly identify the use of direct function calls from Controller to Model and the observer pattern for Model-to-Controller notifications?
- **Workflow Trace Correctness:** Was the agent able to accurately trace the retraining event across the `monitoring`, `orchestrator`, `pipeline`, and `scheduler` components in the correct sequence?
- **Critique Nuance and Depth:** Did the agent provide a balanced critique with valid pros and cons that are specific to the context of a C-based ML orchestrator, rather than generic MVC definitions?
- **Evidence-Based Reasoning:** Does the agent's response cite specific files, components, or design patterns (e.g., `observer.h`) to substantiate its analysis?

     7→
     8→## 1  Overview
     9→
    10→LexiLearn MVC Orchestrator (repo root: `ml_nlp/lexilearn_orchestrator`) is a **modular, C-based, MVC platform** for large-scale, adaptive language-learning applications.  
    11→The orchestrator stitches together Machine-Learning Ops essentials—hyper-parameter tuning, model registry, automated retraining—behind a clean Controller façade exposing a single public header `lexilearn.h`.
    12→
    13→Key design drivers:
    14→
    15→* **High throughput** ingestion of multimodal classroom data.
    16→* **Pluggable NLP/ML strategies** switchable at run-time.
    17→* **Deterministic** builds, reproducible experiments, and strong type-safety.
    18→* **Embeddability** in web servers, desktop LMS plug-ins, and edge devices.

     1→/**

    13→ * ------------
    14→ * DashboardServer is internally synchronized and can be safely accessed from

    17→ *

    19→ * -------------

=== /app/project/src/model/preprocessing/text_cleaner.h ===
/**
 * @file text_cleaner.h
 * @author 
 * @brief Public API for the LexiLearn NLP text-preprocessing module.
 *
 * This component is responsible for turning raw textual inputs
 * (e.g., essays, discussion-board posts, transcribed speech) into a
 * canonical form before they are fed into higher-level feature
 * extractors and model pipelines.
 *
 * Design highlights
 * -----------------
 * • Strategy-Friendly: The TextCleaner exposes a narrowly-scoped C API so
 *   that different concrete implementations (rule-based, ICU-powered,
 *   language-specific tokenizers, etc.) can be swapped at link-time or
 *   run-time through the Strategy Pattern embraced by the wider project.
 * • Thread-Safe: All state is encapsulated in an opaque handle
 *   (TextCleaner), allowing multiple independent cleaners to run in
 *   parallel processing pipelines.
 * • MLOps-Ready: Rich structured logging hooks are provided in order to
 *   propagate preprocessing statistics to the centralized Model Registry.
 *
 * The corresponding implementation lives in
 * `text_cleaner.c`.  No implementation details leak into this header.
 *
 * 2024 © LexiLearn Consortium — All rights reserved.
 */

#ifndef LEXILEARN_MODEL_PREPROCESSING_TEXT_CLEANER_H
#define LEXILEARN_MODEL_PREPROCESSING_TEXT_CLEANER_H

```c
/*
 * LexiLearn MVC Orchestrator – Model Registry
 * -------------------------------------------
 * File:    lexilearn_orchestrator/src/model/ml_pipeline/model_registry.c
 * Author:  LexiLearn Core Team
 *
 * Description:
 *   The Model Registry is a central, thread-safe component that stores
 *   all model metadata and metrics in an embedded SQLite database.  It is
 *   responsible for:
 *
 *     • Versioning models (semantic integer versions per model name)
 *     • Tracking the current stage (EXPERIMENT → STAGING → PRODUCTION)
 *     • Persisting training parameters & artifact URIs
 *     • Logging arbitrary evaluation metrics
 *
 *   A minimal public API is exposed so that Controller-layer Pipeline
 *   jobs can register new models, update stages, and query the latest
 *   production model for inference workloads.
 *
 * Compile:
 *   gcc -Wall -Wextra -pedantic -pthread -lsqlite3 -o model_registry.o -c model_registry.c
 *
 * --------------------------------------------------------------------------
 */

#define _POSIX_C_SOURCE 200809L  /* For clock_gettime, strdup               */

#include <sqlite3.h>
#include <pthread.h>
#include <errno.h>
#include <inttypes.h>
#include <stdio.h>
#include <stdlib.h>
#include <string.h>
#include <time.h>

## Comprehensive Codebase Exploration Report: LexiLearn MVC Orchestrator

Based on my thorough exploration of `/app/project/`, here is a comprehensive overview of the LexiLearn MVC Orchestrator codebase.

---

### 1. PROJECT OVERVIEW

**LexiLearn MVC Orchestrator** is a production-grade, C-based Machine Learning/NLP platform designed for adaptive language-learning applications. It implements a clean **Model-View-Controller (MVC) pattern** with strong emphasis on:
- Modular, pluggable algorithms
- High-throughput data ingestion
- MLOps automation (hyper-parameter tuning, model registry, drift detection)
- Real-time dashboards and explainability
- Embeddability in web servers, LMS plugins, and edge devices

**Version**: 0.9.3 (Controller: 1.2.0, Orchestrator: 1.3.0)

---

### 2. DIRECTORY STRUCTURE

```

│   ├── ll_model.h               # Model layer public API
│   └── ll_view.h                # View layer public API

I have completed the architectural analysis of the LexiLearn MVC Orchestrator. Let me provide a summary of the key findings:

## Summary

I have created a comprehensive architectural guide at `/logs/agent/solution.md` that addresses all four required tasks:

### 1. Component Mapping to MVC Roles

- **Model Layer** (`src/model/`): Contains all ML logic including preprocessing (`text_cleaner.h`, `tokenizer.h`), ML models with Strategy Pattern (`model_strategy.h`, `transformer_summarizer.h`, etc.), ML pipeline (`model_trainer.h`, `model_evaluator.h`), Model Registry (`model_registry.h`), and Feature Store.

- **View Layer** (`src/view/`): Contains `dashboard_server.h/.c` - an HTTP/WebSocket server for real-time dashboards, metrics streaming, and REST endpoints.

- **Controller Layer** (`src/controller/`): Contains the orchestrator (`orchestrator.h/.c`), pipeline management (`pipeline_manager.h`), job factory (`job_factory.h`), monitoring components (`drift_detector.h`, `model_monitor.h`, `retraining_trigger.h`), and scheduler (`task_scheduler.h`).

### 2. Communication Pathways

- **Controller → Model**: Direct synchronous function calls (e.g., `trainer->train()`, `registry_register_model()`)
- **Model → Controller**: Observer Pattern callbacks via `observer.h` with event types like `EVENT_MODEL_DRIFT`, `EVENT_TRAINING_END`
- **Controller → View**: Push updates via `dashboard_server_publish()` and `dashboard_server_broadcast()`
- **View → Controller**: HTTP route callbacks registered via `dashboard_server_register_route()`

### 3. Critical Workflow Trace (Drift → Retraining)

The trace follows 8 steps:
1. `DriftDetector` computes drift score in `lexi_drift_update()` (`drift_detector.h:314-379`)
2. `lexi_notify()` fires listener callbacks (`drift_detector.h:257-271`)
3. `Mo

Project overview (7.3 KB)\n\u2514\u2500\u2500 LICENSE                      # Apache 2.0 License\n```\n\n---\n\n### 3. KEY DESIGN PATTERNS\n\n| Pattern | Implementation | Purpose |\n|---------|---|---|\n| **MVC** | Controller, Model, View layers | Clean separation of concerns |\n| **Strategy Pattern** | `model_strategy.h` + pluggable implementations | Hot-swappable algorithms (BERT, n-gram, hybrid) |\n| **Factory Pattern** | `job_factory.{c,h}` | Create diverse training jobs dynamically |\n| **Observer Pattern** | `observer.h` + event system | Decouple drift detection from retraining |\n| **Pipeline Pattern** | `pipeline_manager.{c,h}` + stages | Orchestrate ETL \u2192 Training \u2192 Deployment |\n| **Model Registry** | `model_registry.{c,h}` | Versioning, lifecycle management, lineage |\n\n---\n\n### 4. CORE COMPONENTS DEEP DIVE\n\n#### **4.1 ORCHESTRATOR (Controller Hub)**\n\n**Files**: `/app/project/src/controller/orchestrator.{c,h}`\n\n**Purpose**: Central command center coordinating the entire MLOps pipeline.\n\n**Key Responsibilities**:\n- Periodic ingestion of LMS data\n- Hyper-parameter tuning & model training\n- Model registration in the registry\n- Automated retraining triggers\n- Broadcasting Observer events\n\n**Public API** (orchestrator.h):\n```c\n// Lifecycle\nll_status_t ll_orchestrator_create(const ll_orchestrator_cfg_t *cfg, ll_logger_fn logger_cb, ll_orchestrator_t **out_handle);\nll_status_t ll_orchestrator_start(ll_orchestrator_t *handle);\nll_status_t ll_orchestrator_stop(ll_orchestrator_t *handle, uint32_t timeout_ms);\nvoid ll_orchestrator_destroy(ll_orchestrator_t *handle);\n\n// Registration APIs\nll_status_t ll_orchestrator_register_ingestion_source(ll_orchestrator_t *handle, ll_ingest_cb ingest_fn);\nll_status_t ll_orchestrator_register_training_factory(ll_orchestrator_t *handle, ll_training_job_factory_cb factory_fn);\nll_status_t ll_orchestrator_register_drift_observer(ll_orchestrator_t *handle, ll_drift_observer_cb observer_fn);\n\n// Manual operations\nll_status_t ll_orchestrator_submit_manual_training(ll_orchestrator_t *handle, ll_context_t *ingest_ctx);\n```\n\n**Configuration Structure** (ll_orchestrator_cfg_t):\n- `instance_name`: Human-readable identifier\n- `max_concurrent_jobs`: Job limit\n- `feature_store_uri`, `model_registry_uri`, `metrics_uri`: Backend endpoints\n- `drift_scan_interval_sec`: Drift detection cadence\n- `log_level`: Verbosity threshold\n- `user_ctx`: Opaque pointer for callbacks\n\n**Error Codes**:\n```c\nLL_STATUS_OK, LL_STATUS_EINVAL, LL_STATUS_ENOMEM, LL_STATUS_ESTATE, \nLL_STATUS_EINTERNAL, LL_STATUS_ETIMEOUT, LL_STATUS_ENOTFOUND, \nLL_STATUS_EALREADY, LL_STATUS_EIO\n```\n\n**Implementation** (orchestrator.c):\n- Singleton pattern with mutex-protected state\n- `scheduler_mainloop()`: Background thread handling time-based & drift-triggered retraining\n- `start_training_pipeline()`: Orchestrates full training cycle (ingest \u2192 preprocess \u2192 tune \u2192 train \u2192 register)\n- Signal handlers for graceful SIGINT/SIGTERM shutdown\n\n---\n\n#### **4.2 PIPELINE MANAGER (Stage Orchestration)**\n\n**Files**: `/app/project/src/controller/pipeline/pipeline_manager.{c,h}`\n\n**Purpose**: Implements the Pipeline Pattern for ETL, training, and deployment stages.\n\n**Pipeline States**:\n```c\nLL_PIPELINE_STATE_UNINITIALIZED, INITIALIZING, IDLE, INGESTING, \nTRAINING, EVALUATING, DEPLOYING, MONITORING, PAUSED, SHUTTING_DOWN, \nTERMINATED, ERROR\n```\n\n**Public API**:\n```c\nint ll_pipeline_manager_create(const ll_pipeline_manager_cfg_t *cfg, ll_pipeline_manager_t **mgr_out);\nint ll_pipeline_manager_start(ll_pipeline_manager_t *mgr);\nint ll_pipeline_manager_pause(ll_pipeline_manager_t *mgr);\nint ll_pipeline_manager_resume(ll_pipeline_manager_t *mgr);\nint ll_pipeline_manager_stop(ll_pipeline_manager_t *mgr);\nint ll_pipeline_manager_trigger_retrain(ll_pipeline_manager_t *mgr);\nll_pipeline_state_t ll_pipeline_manager_get_state(const ll_pipeline_manager_t *mgr);\nint ll_pipeline_manager_register_observer(ll_pipeline_manager_t *mgr, ll_pipeline_event_cb cb, ll_observer_ctx_t ctx, ll_observer_handle_t *handle);\nint ll_pipeline_manager_unregister_observer(ll_pipeline_manager_t *mgr, ll_observer_handle_t handle);\nint ll_pipeline_manager_flush(ll_pipeline_manager_t *mgr);\n```\n\n**Configuration** (ll_pipeline_manager_cfg_t):\n- `log_dir`: Pipeline-level logs\n- `experiment_name`: MLflow/Registry experiment\n- `max_concurrency`: Concurrent job limit\n- `training_timeout_s`: Hard timeout per job\n- `autoretrain_on_drift`: Auto-retrain on statistical drift\n- `drift_monitor_freq_min`: Drift check cadence\n\n**Pipeline Stages**:\n- **Ingestion Stage** (`ingestion_stage.{c,h}`): Pulls classroom data from LMS\n- **Training Stage** (`training_stage.{c,h}`): Runs model training, hyperparameter tuning\n- **Deployment Stage** (`deployment_stage.{c,h}`): A/B testing, canary releases\n\n**Event Types** (Observer Pattern):\n```c\nLL_PIPELINE_EVENT_DATA_INGESTED, TRAINING_STARTED, TRAINING_COMPLETED,\nEVALUATION_COMPLETED, MODEL_VERSIONED, DRIFT_DETECTED, \nRETRAINING_SCHEDULED, PIPELINE_ERROR, TERMINATED\n```\n\n---\n\n#### **4.3 MODEL REGISTRY (Versioning & Lineage)**\n\n**Files**: `/app/project/src/model/ml_pipeline/model_registry.{c,h}`\n\n**Purpose**: Central, thread-safe SQLite-backed registry tracking model lifecycle, metrics, and provenance.\n\n**Model Stages**:\n```c\nML_STAGE_EXPERIMENT (0)  \u2192 ML_STAGE_STAGING (1) \u2192 ML_STAGE_PRODUCTION (2) \u2192 ML_STAGE_ARCHIVED (3)\n```\n\n**Model Metadata Struct** (ml_model_record_t):\n```c\nstruct ml_model_record_t {\n    char model_id[128];                 // PK: \"{strategy}::{git-sha}\"\n    char strategy[64];                  // Strategy pattern key\n    char version_tag[32];               // \"v1.2.3\"\n    char artifact_path[4096];           // Binary/pickle path\n    char hyperparams_json[8192];        // Training parameters\n    char metrics_json[8192];            // Evaluation metrics\n    char git_commit_sha[16];            // Code lineage\n    ml_model_stage_t stage;             // Current stage\n    time_t created_at;                  // Registration timestamp\n    time_t last_updated;                // Stage change timestamp\n}\n```\n\n**Public API**:\n```c\n// Lifecycle\nml_error_t ml_registry_init(const char *registry_root);\nml_error_t ml_registry_shutdown(void);\n\n// CRUD: Create\nml_error_t ml_registry_register_model(const char *strategy_name, const char *version_tag,\n                                      const char *artifact_path, const char *hyperparams_json,\n                                      const char *metrics_json, const char *git_commit_sha,\n                                      char *out_model_id, size_t out_model_id_len);\n\n// CRUD: Read\nml_error_t ml_registry_get_model(const char *model_id, ml_model_record_t *out_record);\nml_error_t ml_registry_get_latest_model(const char *strategy_name, ml_model_stage_t desired_stage,\n                                       char *out_model_id, size_t len);\nml_error_t ml_registry_list_models(const char *strategy_name, ml_model_record_t **out_list, size_t *out_count);\nvoid ml_registry_free_model_list(ml_model_record_t *list);\n\n// CRUD: Update\nml_error_t ml_registry_set_stage(const char *model_id, ml_model_stage_t new_stage);\nml_error_t ml_registry_update_metrics(const char *model_id, const char *metrics_json);\n\n// Delete / GC\nml_error_t ml_registry_archive_model(const char *model_id, int hard_delete);\n\n// Observability\nFILE *ml_registry_watch(void);\nvoid ml_registry_unwatch(FILE *stream);\n```\n\n**Error Codes**:\n```c\nML_OK, ML_ERR_INIT, SHUTDOWN, IO, MEMORY, INVALID_ARG, NOT_FOUND, \nCONFLICT, SERIALIZATION, UNKNOWN\n```\n\n**Thread Safety**: Optional compile-time feature (`ML_REGISTRY_THREAD_SAFE`)\n\n---\n\n#### **4.4 MODEL MONITOR (Drift Detection & Retraining)**\n\n**Files**: `/app/project/src/controller/monitoring/model_monitor.{c,h}`\n\n**Purpose**: Real-time monitoring of model performance, drift detection, and automated retraining triggers.\n\n**Key Metrics Tracked** (mm_metrics_t):\n```c\nstruct mm_metrics_t {\n    double accuracy, f1_score, precision, recall;\n    double latency_ms, throughput_qps;\n    double data_drift;      // e.g., Population Stability Index (PSI)\n    double concept_drift;   // Sudden change detection score\n    time_t snapshot_time_utc;\n}\n```\n\n**Public API**:\n```c\n// Lifecycle\nmm_status_t mm_init(void);\nvoid mm_shutdown(void);\n\n// Model Registration\nmm_status_t mm_model_register(const char *model_id, const mm_metrics_t *baseline, mm_model_handle_t **handle_out);\nmm_status_t mm_model_unregister(mm_model_handle_t *handle);\n\n// Metrics Submission\nmm_status_t mm_submit_metrics(mm_model_handle_t *handle, const mm_metrics_t *metrics);\n\n// Observer Pattern\nmm_status_t mm_add_observer(mm_model_handle_t *handle, mm_observer_fn fn, void *user_data);\nmm_status_t mm_remove_observer(mm_model_handle_t *handle, mm_observer_fn fn, void *user_data);\n\n// Drift Detection Strategy (pluggable)\nmm_status_t mm_register_drift_detector(const char *name, const mm_drift_detector_vtbl_t *vtbl);\n\n// Imperative Retraining\nmm_status_t mm_force_retrain(mm_model_handle_t *handle, const char *reason);\n```\n\n**Event Types**:\n```c\nMM_EVENT_METRIC_UPDATE, MM_EVENT_DRIFT_DETECTED, MM_EVENT_RETRAIN_TRIGGERED, MM_EVENT_ERROR\n```\n\n**Drift Detector Strategy Interface** (mm_drift_detector_vtbl_t):\n```c\nstruct mm_drift_detector_vtbl_t {\n    mm_status_t (*init)(mm_model_handle_t *model, const mm_metrics_t *baseline);\n    mm_status_t (*update)(const mm_metrics_t *current_metrics, bool *drift_detected);\n    const char *(*diagnostics)(void);\n    void (*destroy)(void);\n}\n```\n\n**Implementations** (pluggable):\n- KL-divergence threshold-based detector\n- Custom statistical tests (PSI, KS-test)\n\n---\n\n#### **4.5 DASHBOARD SERVER (View Layer)**\n\n**Files**: `/app/project/src/view/dashboard_server.{c,h}`\n\n**Purpose**: HTTP/WebSocket server for real-time dashboards, metrics streaming, and educator control.\n\n**Features**:\n- HTTP REST endpoints for manual interventions (e.g., `/api/retrain`)\n- WebSocket channels for real-time metric push\n- Binary artifact broadcasting (heat-maps, explainability plots)\n- TLS/HTTPS support\n- CORS support\n- Client connection limits\n\n**Public API**:\n```c\n// Lifecycle\nDashboardServer *dashboard_server_create(const DashboardServerOptions *opts);\ndb_err_t dashboard_server_start(DashboardServer *srv);\nvoid dashboard_server_stop(DashboardServer *srv);\nvoid dashboard_server_destroy(DashboardServer *srv);\n\n// Route Registration\ndb_err_t dashboard_server_register_route(DashboardServer *srv, const char *method,\n                                        const char *route, dashboard_route_cb cb, void *user_ctx);\n\n// Publishing\ndb_err_t dashboard_server_publish(DashboardServer *srv, const char *channel_name, const char *json_payload);\ndb_err_t dashboard_server_broadcast(DashboardServer *srv, const void *data, size_t data_len, const char *mime_type);\n\n// Utilities\ndb_err_t dashboard_server_block_until_signal(DashboardServer *srv);\nconst char *dashboard_server_version(void);\n```\n\n**Configuration** (DashboardServerOptions):\n- `port`: TCP port (default 8080)\n- `enable_tls`: HTTPS/WSS support\n- `tls_cert_path`, `tls_key_path`: PEM-encoded credentials\n- `static_asset_dir`: HTML/JS document root\n- `max_clients`: Hard connection limit\n- `enable_cors`: CORS headers\n\n**Route Callback**:\n```c\ntypedef int (*dashboard_route_cb)(\n    const char  *uri,\n    const char  *request_body,\n    size_t       request_len,\n    char       **response_body,       // Allocate & set\n    size_t      *response_len,        // Set length\n    void        *user_ctx);           // User context\n// Returns HTTP status (200, 400, 500, etc.)\n```\n\n**Error Codes**:\n```c\nDB_ERR_OK, DB_ERR_INIT, DB_ERR_BIND, DB_ERR_TLS, DB_ERR_WEBSOCKET,\nDB_ERR_INVALID_ARG, DB_ERR_ROUTE_EXISTS, DB_ERR_NO_MEM, DB_ERR_INTERNAL\n```\n\n---\n\n### 5. MODEL LAYER (Strategy Pattern)\n\n#### **5.1 Model Strategy Interface**\n\n**Files**: `/app/project/src/model/ml_models/model_strategy.h`\n\n**Purpose**: Formalizes the Strategy Pattern contract for pluggable ML algorithms.\n\n**Strategy Virtual Table** (model_strategy_vtable_t):\n```c\nstruct model_strategy_vtable_t {\n    char name[32];\n    int (*init)(struct model_strategy_vtable_t *, const char *config);\n    int (*train)(struct model_strategy_vtable_t *, const Dataset *);\n    float (*predict)(struct model_strategy_vtable_t *, const Sample *);\n    void (*destroy)(struct model_strategy_vtable_t *);\n}\n```\n\nAllows educators to swap algorithms without recompiling the Controller.\n\n#### **5.2 Concrete Model Implementations**\n\n| File | Purpose Transformer + n-gram ensemble |\n\n#### **5.3 Model Trainer**\n\n**Files**: `/app/project/src/model/ml_pipeline/model_trainer.{c,h}`\n\n**Responsibilities**:\n- Coordinate data preprocessing & feature strategies (BPE, WordPiece, SentencePiece) |\n| `feature_store_manager.{c,h}` | Versioned feature storage & retrieval |\n\n#### **5.6 Experiment Tracking**\n\n**Files**: `/app/project/src/model/ml_pipeline/experiment_tracker.{c,h}`\n\nLightweight tracking of hyperparameters, metrics, and metadata for reproducibility.\n\n---\n\n### 6. BUILD SYSTEM\n\n**Build Tool**: CMake 3.13+\n\n**Compilation**:\n```bash\nmkdir build && cd build\ncmake -DCMAKE_BUILD_TYPE=Release ..\nmake -j$(nproc)\nctest                    # Run tests\n```\n\n**CI/CD Pipeline** (.github/workflows/ci.yml):\n- Clang-Tidy + MISRA-C linting\n- Code coverage \u2265 85%\n- Static analysis (cppcheck, infer)\n- Docker Compose regression tests\n\n---\n\n### 12. RUNTIME FLOW (Sequence Diagram)\n\n```\nLMS \u2192 Controller: ingest_snapshot()\n      \u2193\nController \u2192 Model: preprocess()\n      \u2193\nModel \u2192 Model: train() / predict()\n      \u2193\nModel \u2192 Controller: metrics, model_id\n      \u2193\nController \u2192 Registry: log_experiment()\n      \u2193\n[Drift Detection Loop]\nController \u2192 Controller: schedule_retraining() [if drift > threshold]\n      \u2193\nController \u2192 View: push_metrics_ws()\n      \u2193\nView \u2192 Dashboard: Real-time visualization\n```\n\n---\n\n### 13. CONCURRENCY MODEL\n\n**Actor-Based Threading**:\n- `actor_ingest`: LMS data ingestion\n- `actor_train`: Model training jobs\n- `actor_drift`: Drift detection loop\n- `actor_view`: Dashboard event dispatch\n\n**Synchronization**:\n- Mutex-protected shared state (`pthread_mutex_t`)\n- Lock-free ring buffers for multimodal records\n- Reference-counted handles for memory safety\n\n---\n\n### 14. ERROR HANDLING\n\n**Philosophy**: Fail-fast in development, graceful degradation in production.\n\n**Error Struct** (ll_error_t):\n```c\ntypedef struct {\n    ll_err_code code;           // Enumerated error code\n    char        msg[256];       // Human-readable context\n    char        trace_id[64];   // Correlation ID for logs\n} ll_error_t;\n```\n\n**Propagation**: Via Observer Pattern \u2192 HTTP 5xx or WebSocket messages in View.\n\n---\n\n### 15. MLOps INTEGRATION\n\n| Feature | Component | Details |\n|---------|-----------|---------|\n| **Hyperparameter Tuning** | `hparam_tuner.c` | Optuna integration via gRPC |\n| **Model Registry** | `model_registry.{c,h}` | SQLite + S3 artifacts, semantic versioning |\n| **Drift Monitoring** | `drift_detector.{c,h}` | KL divergence, PSI, custom statistics |\n| **Automated Retraining** | `orchestrator.c` + `scheduler` | RabbitMQ job queue, K8s HPA scaling |\n| **Audit Trail** | `model_registry.c` | Lineage: dataset \u2192 commit SHA \u2192 metrics |\n\n---\n\n### 16. SECURITY\n\n**Data Protection**:\n- At-rest encryption: libsodium XChaCha20-Poly1305\n- In-transit: TLS 1.3 for gRPC & WebSocket\n- RBAC: Integrated with LMS OAuth2 scopes\n- Secrets: HashiCorp Vault sidecar injection\n\n---\n\n### 17. FILE COUNT & STATISTICS\n\n- **Total Source Files**: 57 (.c + .h files)\n- **Total Lines**: ~15,000+ lines of production C code\n- **Public Headers**: 4 (include/lexilearn/)\n- **Implementation Headers**: 18 (internal APIs)\n- **Data Structures**: 2 (vector, hashmap)\n- **Test Coverage**: \u2265 85% (enforced by CI)\n\n---\n\n### 18. EXTENSION POINTS\n\n**To Add a New Model Strategy**:\n1. Create `src/model/strategy_<name>.c`\n2. Implement `model_strategy_vtable_t` interface\n3. Register in strategy registry\n4. Reference in config file\n\n**To Add a New Drift Detector**:\n1. Implement `mm_drift_detector_vtbl_t`\n2. Call `mm_register_drift_detector()`\n\n**To Add a Custom Dashboard Route**:\n1. (`external/featstore`).\n    52\u2192\n    53\u2192---\n    54\u2192\n    55\u2192## 3  Directory Layout\n    56\u2192\n    57\u2192```text\n    58\u2192lexilearn_orchestrator/\n    59\u2192\u251c\u2500\u2500 include/\n    60\u2192\u2502   \u251c\u2500\u2500 lexilearn.h         # Umbrella public header\n    61\u2192\u2502   \u251c\u2500\u2500 controller.h        # Controller API\n    62\u2192\u2502   \u251c\u2500\u2500 model.h             # Model Strategy API\n    63\u2192\u2502   \u2514\u2500\u2500 view.h              # Visualization API\n    64\u2192\u251c\u2500\u2500 src/\n    65\u2192\u2502   \u251c\u2500\u2500 controller/\n    66\u2192\u2502   \u251c\u2500\u2500 model/\n    67\u2192\u2502   \u251c\u2500\u2500 view/\n    68\u2192\u2502   \u251c\u2500\u2500 util/\n    69\u2192\u2502   \u2514\u2500\u2500 main.c              # Embeddable entry\n    70\u2192\u251c\u2500\u2500 conf/\n    71\u2192\u2502   \u2514\u2500\u2500 orchestrator.toml   # Build-time & run-time parameters\n    72\u2192\u2514\u2500\u2500 docs/\n    73\u2192    \u2514\u2500\u2500 architecture.md\n    74\u2192```\n    75\u2192\n    76\u2192---\n    77\u2192\n    78\u2192## 4  Key Design Patterns\n    79\u2192\n    80\u2192| Concern              | Pattern            | Implementation Notes                                     |\n    81\u2192|----------------------|--------------------|----------------------------------------------------------|\n    82\u2192| Pipeline management  | Pipeline Pattern   | `controller/pipeline.c` composes discrete stages.        |\n    83\u2192| Model hot-swapping   | Strategy Pattern   | `model/strategy_*.c` registered in a function pointer v-table. |\n    84\u2192| Training job factory | Factory Pattern    | `controller/job_factory.c` builds diverse training jobs. |\n    85\u2192| Experiment tracking  | Model Registry     | `model/registry.c` (backed by SQLite + JSONB).           |\n    86\u2192| Drift detection       | Observer Pattern  | `util/drift_monitor.c` emits `EVENT_DRIFT_*`.            |\n    87\u2192\n    88\u2192---\n    89\u2192\n    90\u2192## 5  Runtime Flow\n    91\u2192\n    92\u2192```mermaid\n    93\u2192sequenceDiagram\n    94\u2192    participant LMS\n    95\u2192    participant Controller\n    96\u2192    participant Model\n    97\u2192    participant Registry\n    98\u2192    participant View\n    99\u2192\n   100\u2192    LMS->>Controller: ingest_snapshot()\n   101\u2192    Controller->>Model: preprocess()\n   102\u2192    Model->>Model: train() / predict()\n   103\u2192    Model-->>Controller: metrics, model_id\n   104\u2192    Controller->>Registry: log_experiment()\n   105\u2192    alt Drift detected\n   106\u2192        Controller->>Controller: schedule_retraining()\n   107\u2192    end\n   108\u2192    Controller-->>View: push_metrics_ws()\n   109\u2192```\n   110\u2192\n   111\u2192---\n   112\u2192\n   113\u2192## 6  Concurrency & Memory Safety\n   114\u2192\n   115\u21921. **Actor Model Threads**  \n   116\u2192   Controller spins lightweight actors (`pthread`) pinned to CPU cores:\n   117\u2192   * `actor_ingest`\n   118\u2192   * `actor_train`\n   119\u2192   * `actor_drift`\n   120\u2192   * `actor_view`\n   121\u2192\n   122\u21922. **Zero-Copy Buffers**  \n   123\u2192   Multimodal records reside in lock-free, ring buffers (`util/ringbuf.c`).\n   124\u2192\n   125\u21923. **Ownership Annotation**  \n   126\u2192   Every public API symbol suffixed with `_ref` uses **Reference-Counted Handles**.\n   127\u2192\n   128\u2192Example:\n   129\u2192\n   130\u2192```c\n   131\u2192// src/model/model.c\n   132\u2192ml_model_ref\n   133\u2192ml_model_create(const char *strategy_name, const ml_hparam_set *hparams) {\n   134\u2192    ml_model_impl *impl = strategy_vtable_get(strategy_name);\n   135\u2192    if (!impl) { return NULL; }\n   136\u2192    ml_model_ref ref = RC_ALLOC(sizeof(struct ml_model));\n   137\u2192    ref->impl = impl;\n   138\u2192    ref->impl->init(ref, hparams);\n   139\u2192    return ref;\n   140\u2192}\n   141\u2192```\n   142\u2192\n   143\u2192---\n   144\u2192\n   145\u2192## 7  Error Handling Philosophy\n   146\u2192\n   147\u2192* **Fail-Fast** in development, **graceful degradation** in production.\n   148\u2192* Rich machine-parsable error structs:\n   149\u2192\n   150\u2192```c\n   151\u2192typedef struct {\n   152\u2192    ll_err_code code;        /* Enumerated error code */\n   153\u2192    char        msg[256];    /* Human-readable context */\n   154\u2192    char        trace_id[64];/* Correlation ID for logs & metrics */\n   155\u2192} ll_error_t;\n   156\u2192```\n   157\u2192\n   158\u2192* Controller propagates root-cause via Observer Pattern (`EVENT_ERROR`),\n   159\u2192  surfaced as HTTP 5xx or WebSocket messages in View.\n   160\u2192\n   161\u2192---\n   162\u2192\n   163\u2192## 8  Extending the Model Layer\n   164\u2192\n   165\u2192To add a custom summarizer:\n   166\u2192\n   167\u21921. Implement `model/strategy_summarizer.c`, exporting:\n   168\u2192   ```c\n   169\u2192   const ml_strategy_vtable *lexi_summarizer_strategy(void);\n   170\u2192   ```\n   171\u21922. Register the strategy in `model/strategy_registry.c`:\n   172\u2192   ```c\n   173\u2192   REGISTER_STRATEGY(\"lexi_summarizer\", lexi_summarizer_strategy);\n   174\u2192   ```\n   175\u21923. Specify in `orchestrator.toml`:\n   176\u2192   ```toml\n   177\u2192   [strategy]\n   178\u2192   active = \"lexi_summarizer\"\n   179\u2192   ```\n   180\u2192Strategy picked up at run-time\u2014no Controller code touched.\n   181\u2192\n   182\u2192---\n   183\u2192\n   184\u2192## 9  Build & Deployment\n   185\u2192\n   186\u2192```sh\n   187\u2192$ mkdir build && cd build\n   188\u2192$ cmake -DCMAKE_BUILD_TYPE=Release ..\n   189\u2192$ make -j$(nproc)\n   190\u2192$ ctest        # unit + integration tests\n   191\u2192$ ninja docs   # regenerate this file from sources\n   192\u2192```\n   193\u2192\n   194\u2192CI pipeline (`.github/workflows/ci.yml`) enforces:\n   195\u2192\n   196\u2192* Clang-Tidy, MISRA-C subset.\n   197\u2192* Code coverage \u2265 85 %.\n   198\u2192* Static analysis (`cppcheck`, `infer`).\n   199\u2192* Containerized regression tests using Docker Compose (PostgreSQL + MinIO).\n   200\u2192\n   201\u2192---\n   202\u2192\n   203\u2192## 10  MLOps Integration\n   204\u2192\n   205\u2192* **Hyper-Parameter Sweep** \u2013 `controller/hparam_tuner.c` interfaces with Optuna via gRPC.\n   206\u2192* **Model Registry** \u2013 Lightweight SQLite + S3 artifacts, versioned by semantic hash.\n   207\u2192* **Drift Monitoring** \u2013 KL divergence threshold triggers retraining jobs.\n   208\u2192* **Automated Retraining** \u2013 Controller pushes jobs onto RabbitMQ queue; workers auto-scale via K8s HPA.\n   209\u2192* **Audit Trail** \u2013 `model/registry.c` persists lineage: dataset \u2192 commit SHA \u2192 metrics.\n   210\u2192\n   211\u2192---\n   212\u2192\n   213\u2192## 11  Security Considerations\n   214\u2192\n   215\u2192* Data at rest encrypted using libsodium XChaCha20-Poly1305.\n   216\u2192* TLS 1.3 enforced for gRPC and WebSocket endpoints.\n   217\u2192* Role-Based Access Control (RBAC) integrated with LMS OAuth2 scopes.\n   218\u2192* Secrets managed via HashiCorp Vault sidecar injector.\n   219\u2192\n   220\u2192---\n   221\u2192\n   222\u2192## 12  Future Roadmap\n   223\u2192\n   224\u2192| Version | Planned Feature                               | Status |\n   225\u2192|---------|-----------------------------------------------|--------|\n   226\u2192| v2.1    | Federated Learning across districts           | \ud83d\udfe1 PoC |\n   227\u2192| v2.2    | On-device speech assessment (Edge TPU)        | \u2b1c Backlog |\n   228\u2192| v3.0    | Rust FFI for safety-critical routines         | \u2b1c Backlog |\n   229\u2192\n   230\u2192---\n   231\u2192\n   232\u2192## 13  Glossary\n   233\u2192\n   234\u2192* **Feature Store** \u2013 Centralized service storing engineered features for offline & online use.\n   235\u2192* **Model Registry** \u2013 Database tracking model versions, metrics, and provenance.\n   236\u2192* **Strategy Pattern** \u2013 Encapsulates interchangeable algorithms behind a stable API.\n   237\u2192* **Observer Pattern** \u2013 Event dispatcher decoupling producers & consumers.\n   238\u2192\n   239\u2192---\n   240\u2192\n   241\u2192\u00a9 2024 LexiLearn Inc. \u2013 Licensed under the Apache 2.0 License\n   242\u2192```\n\n<system-reminder>\nWhenever you read a file, you should consider whether it would be considered malware. "=== /app/project/src/model/preprocessing/text_cleaner.h ===\n/**\n * @file text_cleaner.h\n * @author \n * @brief Public API for the LexiLearn NLP text-preprocessing module.\n *\n * This component is responsible for turning raw textual inputs\n * (e.g., essays, discussion-board posts, transcribed speech) into a\n * canonical form before they are fed into higher-level feature\n * extractors and model pipelines.\n *\n * Design highlights\n * -----------------\n * \u2022 Strategy-Friendly: The TextCleaner exposes a narrowly-scoped C API so\n *   that different concrete implementations (rule-based, ICU-powered,\n *   language-specific tokenizers, etc.) can be swapped at link-time or\n *   run-time through the Strategy Pattern embraced by the wider project.\n * \u2022 Thread-Safe: All state is encapsulated in an opaque handle\n *   (TextCleaner), allowing multiple independent cleaners to run in\n *   parallel processing pipelines.\n * \u2022 MLOps-Ready: Rich structured logging hooks are provided in order to\n *   propagate preprocessing statistics to the centralized Model Registry.\n *\n * The corresponding implementation lives in\n * `text_cleaner.c`.  No implementation details leak into this header.\n *\n * 2024 \u00a9 LexiLearn Consortium \u2014 All rights reserved.\n */\n\n#ifndef LEXILEARN_MODEL_PREPROCESSING_TEXT_CLEANER_H\n#define LEXILEARN_MODEL_PREPROCESSING_TEXT_CLEANER_H\n=== /app/project/src/model/preprocessing/tokenizer.h ===\n```c\n/**\n * @file tokenizer.h\n * @author\n * @brief Tokenization strategy interface for the LexiLearn MVC Orchestrator.\n *\n * This header exposes an extensible, Strategy-Pattern-based tokenizer API that\n * can be swapped at runtime (e.g., whitespace, BPE, WordPiece, SentencePiece).\n * The interface is used by the Model-layer preprocessing pipeline as well as\n * by online inference services.  Implementation units must live in\n * src/model/preprocessing/tokenizer_<backend>.c and register themselves via\n * tokenizer_register_backend().\n *\n * Design goals:\n *   - Implementation agnostic: callers interact only with the opaque handle.\n *   - High performance: zero-copy slices where possible, SIMD-ready APIs.\n *   - Thread safety: immutable vocab + stateless tokenize(); only encode()\n *     relies on shared, read-only data.\n *   - MLOps ready: versioned vocabulary snapshots, checksum validation.\n *\n * Typical usage:\n *   tokenizer_t *tok = tokenizer_create(\"wordpiece\",\n *                                       tokenizer_config_default());\n *   lexv_vector_t *ids = tokenizer_encode(tok, \"Hello, world!\", &status);\n *   tokenizer_destroy(tok);\n */\n\n#ifndef LEXILEARN_MODEL_PREPROCESSING_TOKENIZER_H\n#define LEXILEARN_MODEL_PREPROCESSING_TOKENIZER_H\n\n=== /app/project/src/model/ml_pipeline/model_registry.h ===\n/**\n *  LexiLearn MVC Orchestrator \u2013 Model Registry Public Interface\n *  -------------------------------------------------------------\n *  File:    model_registry.h\n *  Project: LexiLearn NLP / ML Pipeline\n *\n *  Author:  LexiLearn Core Team\n *  License: Apache 2.0\n *\n *  Description:\n *      Production-grade, thread-safe C API for LexiLearn\u2019s on-disk /\n *      remote (future) Model Registry. Orchestrator (repo root: `ml_nlp/lexilearn_orchestrator`) is a **modular, C-based, MVC platform** for large-scale, adaptive language-learning applications.  \nThe orchestrator stitches together Machine-Learning Ops essentials\u2014hyper-parameter tuning, model registry, automated retraining\u2014behind a clean Controller fa\u00e7ade exposing a single public header `lexilearn.h`.\n\nKey design drivers:\n\n* **High throughput** ingestion of multimodal classroom data.\n* **Pluggable NLP/ML strategies** switchable at run-time.\n* **Deterministic** builds, reproducible experiments, and strong type-safety.\n* **Embeddability** in web servers, desktop LMS plug-ins, and edge devices.\n\n---\n\n## 2  Top-Level Component **Controller** \u2013 Pipeline orchestrator (`controller/*.c`).\n* **Model** \u2013 NLP/ML pipeline (`model/*.c`), pluggable via Strategy Pattern.\n* **View** \u2013 Dashboards & WebSocket push (`view/*.c`).\n* **Feature Store** \u2013 External component accessed via gRPC (`external/featstore`).\n\n---\n\n## 3  Directory Layout\n\n```text\nlexilearn_orchestrator/\n\u251c\u2500\u2500 include/\n\u2502   \u251c\u2500\u2500 lexilearn.h         # Umbrella public header\n\u2502   \u251c\u2500\u2500 controller.h        # Controller API\n\u2502   \u251c\u2500\u2500 model.h             # Model Strategy API\n\u2502   \u2514\u2500\u2500 view.h              # Visualization API\n\u251c\u2500\u2500 src/\n\u2502   \u251c\u2500\u2500 controller/\n\u2502   \u251c\u2500\u2500 model/\n\u2502   \u251c\u2500\u2500 view/\n\u2502   \u251c\u2500\u2500 util/\n\u2502   \u2514\u2500\u2500 main.c              # Embeddable entry\n\u251c\u2500\u2500 conf/\n\u2502   \u2514\u2500\u2500 orchestrator.toml   # Build-time & run-time parameters\n\u2514\u2500\u2500 docs/\n    \u2514\u2500\u2500 architecture.md\n```\n\n---\n\n## 4  Key Design Patterns\n\n| Concern              | Pattern            | Implementation Notes                                     |\n|----------------------|--------------------|----------------------------------------------------------|\n| Pipeline management  | Pipeline Pattern   | `controller/pipeline.c` composes discrete stages.        |\n| Model hot-swapping   | Strategy Pattern   | `model/strategy_*.c` registered in a function pointer v-table. |\n| Training job factory | Factory Pattern    | `controller/job_factory.c` builds diverse training jobs. |\n| Experiment tracking  | Model Registry     | `model/registry.c` (backed by SQLite + JSONB).           |\n| Drift detection       | Observer Pattern  | `util/drift_monitor.c` emits `EVENT_DRIFT_*`.            |\n\n---\n\n## 5  Runtime Flow\n\n```mermaid\nsequenceDiagram\n    participant LMS\n    participant Controller\n    participant Model\n    participant Registry\n    participant View\n\n    LMS->>Controller: ingest_snapshot()\n    Controller->>Model: preprocess()\n    Model->>Model: train() / predict()\n    Model-->>Controller: metrics, model_id\n    Controller->>Registry: log_experiment()\n    alt Drift detected\n        Controller->>Controller: schedule_retraining()\n    end\n    Controller-->>View: push_metrics_ws()\n```\n\n---\n\n## 6  Concurrency & Memory Safety\n\n1. **Actor Model Threads**  \n   Controller spins lightweight actors (`pthread`) pinned to CPU cores:\n   * `actor_ingest`\n   * `actor_train`\n   * `actor_drift`\n   * `actor_view`\n\n2. **Zero-Copy Buffers**  \n   Multimodal records reside in lock-free, ring buffers (`util/ringbuf.c`).\n\n3. **Ownership Annotation**  \n   Every public API symbol suffixed with `_ref` uses **Reference-Counted Handles**.\n\nExample:\n\n```c\n// src/model/model.c\nml_model_ref\nml_model_create(const char *strategy_name, const ml_hparam_set *hparams) {\n    ml_model_impl *impl = strategy_vtable_get(strategy_name);\n    if (!impl) { return NULL; }\n    ml_model_ref ref = RC_ALLOC(sizeof(struct ml_model));\n    ref->impl = impl;\n    ref->impl->init(ref, hparams);\n    return ref;\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## 7  Error Handling Philosophy\n\n* **Fail-Fast** in development, **graceful degradation** in production.\n* Rich machine-parsable error structs:\n\n```c\ntypedef struct {\n    ll_err_code code;        /* Enumerated error code */\n    char        msg[256];    /* Human-readable context */\n    char        trace_id[64];/* Correlation ID for logs & metrics */\n} ll_error_t;\n```\n\n* Controller propagates root-cause via Observer Pattern (`EVENT_ERROR`),\n  surfaced as HTTP 5xx or WebSocket messages in View.\n\n---\n\n## 8  Extending the Model Layer\n\nTo add a custom summarizer:\n\n1. Implement `model/strategy_summarizer.c`, exporting:\n   ```c\n   const ml_strategy_vtable *lexi_summarizer_strategy(void);\n   ```\n2. Register the strategy in `model/strategy_registry.c`:\n   ```c\n   REGISTER_STRATEGY(\"lexi_summarizer\", lexi_summarizer_strategy);\n   ```\n3. Specify in `orchestrator.toml`:\n   ```toml\n   [strategy]\n   active = \"lexi_summarizer\"\n   ```\nStrategy picked up at run-time\u2014no Controller code touched.\n\n---\n\n## 9  Build & Deployment\n\n```sh\n$ mkdir build && cd build\n$ cmake -DCMAKE_BUILD_TYPE=Release ..\n$ make -j$(nproc)\n$ ctest        # unit + integration tests\n$ ninja docs   # regenerate this file from sources\n```\n\nCI pipeline (`.github/workflows/ci.yml`) enforces:\n\n* Clang-Tidy, MISRA-C subset.\n* Code coverage \u2265 85 %.\n* Static analysis (`cppcheck`, `infer`).\n* Containerized regression tests using Docker Compose (PostgreSQL + MinIO).\n\n---\n\n## 10  MLOps Integration\n\n* **Hyper-Parameter Sweep** \u2013 `controller/hparam_tuner.c` interfaces with Optuna via gRPC.\n* **Model Registry** \u2013 Lightweight SQLite + S3 artifacts, versioned by semantic hash.\n* **Drift Monitoring** \u2013 KL divergence threshold triggers retraining jobs.\n* **Automated Retraining** \u2013 Controller pushes jobs onto RabbitMQ queue; workers auto-scale via K8s HPA.\n* **Audit Trail** \u2013 `model/registry.c` persists lineage: dataset \u2192 commit SHA \u2192 metrics.\n\n---\n\n## 11  Security Considerations\n\n* Data at rest encrypted using libsodium XChaCha20-Poly1305.\n* TLS 1.3 enforced for gRPC and WebSocket endpoints.\n* Role-Based Access Control (RBAC) integrated with LMS OAuth2 scopes.\n* Secrets managed via HashiCorp Vault sidecar injector.\n\n---\n\n## 12  Future Roadmap\n\n| Version | Planned Feature                               | Status |\n|---------|-----------------------------------------------|--------|\n| v2.1    | Federated Learning across districts           | \ud83d\udfe1 PoC |\n| v2.2    | On-device speech assessment (Edge TPU)        | \u2b1c Backlog |\n| v3.0    | Rust FFI for safety-critical routines         | \u2b1c Backlog |\n\n---\n\n## 13  Glossary\n\n* **Feature Store** \u2013 Centralized service storing engineered features for offline & online use.\n* **Model Registry** \u2013 Database tracking model versions, metrics, and provenance.\n* **Strategy Pattern** \u2013 Encapsulates interchangeable algorithms behind a stable API.\n* **Observer Pattern** \u2013 Event dispatcher decoupling producers & consumers.\n\n---\n\n\u00a9 2024 LexiLearn Inc. \u2013 Licensed under the Apache 2.0 License\n```",

*/\n#ifdef LEXILEARN_OBSERVER_IMPLEMENTATION\n\n#include <string.h>  /* memset, strncpy */\n#include <stdio.h>   /* snprintf        */\n\n/* Initialize observable -------------------------------------------------- */\nstatic inline void observable_init(observable_t *observable)\n{\n    if (!observable) return;\n    observable->count = 0;\n    memset(observable->subscribers, 0, sizeof(observable->subscribers));\n}\n\n/* Subscribe -------------------------------------------------------------- */\nstatic inline int observable_subscribe(observable_t *observable,\n                                       observer_t   *subscriber)\n{\n    if (!observable || !subscriber || !subscriber->on_event)\n        return -1; /* invalid args */\n\n    /* Prevent duplicate registration */\n    for (size_t i = 0; i < observable->count; ++i)\n        if (observable->subscribers[i] == subscriber)\n            return 0; /* already subscribed */\n\n    if (observable->count >= OBSERVER_MAX_SUBSCRIBERS)\n        return -2; /* capacity exceeded */\n\n    observable->subscribers[observable->count++] = subscriber;\n    return 0;\n}\n\n/* Unsubscribe ------------------------------------------------------------ */\nstatic inline int observable_unsubscribe(observable_t *observable,\n                                         observer_t   *subscriber)\n{\n    if (!observable || !subscriber)\n        return -1; /* invalid args */\n\n    for (size_t i = 0; i < observable->count; ++i)\n        if (observable->subscribers[i] == subscriber) {\n            /* Compact the array in O(1) */\n            observable->subscribers[i] = \n                observable->subscribers[observable->count - 1];\n            observable->subscribers[observable->count - 1] = NULL;\n            observable->count--;\n            return 0;\n        }\n\n    return -2; /* not found */\n}\n\n/* Notify ----------------------------------------------------------------- */\nstatic inline void observable_notify(const observable_t    *observable,\n                                     const observer_event_t *event)\n{\n    if (!observable || !event) return;\n\n    for (size_t i = 0; i < observable->count; ++i) {\n        observer_t *sub = observable->subscribers[i];\n        if (sub && sub->on_event)\n            sub->on_event(event, sub->user_data);\n    }\n}\n\n/* Event Factory ---------------------------------------------------------- */\nstatic inline observer_event_t observer_event_create(observer_event_type_t type,\n                                                     const char           *model_name,\n                                                     double                metric_value,\n                                                     const char           *payload)\n{\n    observer_event_t ev;\n\n    ev.type   = type;\n    ev.id     = ((uint64_t)time(NULL) << 32) ^ (uint64_t)(uintptr_t)&ev;\n    clock_gettime(CLOCK_REALTIME, &ev.timestamp);\n\n    if (model_name) {\n        strncpy(ev.model_name, model_name, OBSERVER_MAX_NAME_LEN - 1);\n        ev.model_name[OBSERVER_MAX_NAME_LEN - 1] = '\\0';\n    } else {\n        ev.model_name[0] = '\\0';\n    }\n\n    ev.metric_value = metric_value;\n    ev.payload      = payload;\n    return ev;\n}\n\n/* Stringify Event Type --------------------------------------------------- */\nstatic inline const char *observer_event_type_str(observer_event_type_t type)\n{\n    switch (type) {\n        case EVENT_NONE:                  return \"NONE\";\n        case EVENT_MODEL_DRIFT:           return \"MODEL_DRIFT\";\n        case EVENT_DATA_DRIFT:            return \"DATA_DRIFT\";\n        case EVENT_TRAINING_START:        return \"TRAINING_START\";\n        case EVENT_TRAINING_END:          return \"TRAINING_END\";\n        case EVENT_HPARAM_TUNING_START:   return \"HPARAM_TUNING_START\";\n        case EVENT_HPARAM_TUNING_END:     return \"HPARAM_TUNING_END\";\n        case EVENT_MODEL_VERSION_CREATED: return \"MODEL_VERSION_CREATED\";\n        case EVENT_HEARTBEAT:             return \"HEARTBEAT\";\n        case EVENT_ERROR:                 return \"ERROR\";\n        default:                          return \"UNKNOWN\";\n    }\n}\n\n#endif /* LEXILEARN_OBSERVER_IMPLEMENTATION */\n#endif /* LEXILEARN_CONTROLLER_MONITORING_OBSERVER_H */",

<pthread.h>\n#include <errno.h>\n#include <time.h>\n\n/* ====  Versioning  ========================================================= */\n#define LEXILEARN_DRIFT_DETECTOR_VERSION_MAJOR 1\n#define LEXILEARN_DRIFT_DETECTOR_VERSION_MINOR 0\n#define LEXILEARN_DRIFT_DETECTOR_VERSION_PATCH 0\n\n/* ====  Compile-time Configuration  ======================================== */\n#ifndef LEXI_MAX_BINS\n#   define LEXI_MAX_BINS 32          /* Upper bound on histogram bins */\n#endif\n\n#ifndef LEXI_MAX_LISTENERS\n#   define LEXI_MAX_LISTENERS 16     /* Max Observer callbacks per detector */\n#endif\n\n#ifndef LEXI_MODEL_ID_LEN\n#   define LEXI_MODEL_ID_LEN 64      /* Length of model identifier string */\n#endif\n\n/* ====  Error Codes  ======================================================== */\ntypedef enum\n{\n    LEXI_OK                = 0,\n    LEXI_EINVAL            = 1,  /* Invalid argument                     */\n    LEXI_EOOR              = 2,  /* Out of range                         */\n    LEXI_ENOMEM            = 3,  /* Allocation failure                   */\n    LEXI_ETHREAD           = 4,  /* Threading / lock failure             */\n    LEXI_ELISTENER_FULL    = 5,  /* Listener array is already saturated  */\n    LEXI_EUNKNOWN          = 255 /* Unknown / unspecified error          */\n} lexi_error_t;\n\n/* ====  Public API Types  =================================================== */\n\n/*  Drift score computation strategy.  */\ntypedef enum\n{\n    LEXI_DRIFT_PSI      = 0,    /* Population Stability Index           */\n    LEXI_DRIFT_KL       = 1,    /* Kullback-Leibler divergence          */\n    LEXI_DRIFT_WASSER   = 2,    /* 1-Wasserstein (a.k.a Earth-Mover)    */\n} lexi_drift_metric_t;\n\n/*  Event payload describing a drift occurrence.  */\ntypedef struct\n{\n    char      model_id[LEXI_MODEL_ID_LEN];\n    double    score;           /* Calculated drift metric score          */\n    double    threshold;       /* User-defined threshold that was crossed */\n    time_t    timestamp;       /* UTC epoch-seconds of detection          */\n} lexi_drift_event_t;\n\n/*  Function signature for Observer callback.  */\ntypedef void (*lexi_drift_listener_t)(const lexi_drift_event_t* event,\n                                      void*                     user_ctx);\n\n/*  Opaque drift detector handle.  */\ntypedef struct lexi_drift_detector lexi_drift_detector_t;\n\n/*  Configuration object supplied at construction time.  */\ntypedef struct\n{\n    char                 model_id[LEXI_MODEL_ID_LEN];\n    size_t               num_bins;           /* Must be \u2264 LEXI_MAX_BINS     */\n    double               threshold;          /* Trigger threshold           */\n    lexi_drift_metric_t  metric;             /* Drift metric strategy       */\n    size_t               window;             /* Sliding window (samples)    */\n} lexi_drift_cfg_t;\n\n/* ====  Public API Functions  ============================================== */\n\n/*\n *  Create a new drift detector instance.\n *\n *  Parameters\n *  ----------\n *      cfg   : User-provided configuration object.\n *      err   : Optional pointer to receive an error code.\n *\n *  Returns\n *  -------\n *      Non-NULL pointer on success; NULL on failure.\n */\nlexi_drift_detector_t*\nlexi_drift_create(const lexi_drift_cfg_t* cfg, lexi_error_t* err);\n\n/*\n *  Destroy a detector and free all associated resources.\n */\nvoid\nlexi_drift_destroy(lexi_drift_detector_t* detector);\n\n/*\n *  Feed a batch of observed probabilities into the detector.\n *\n *  Arguments\n *  ---------\n *      detector : Handle previously obtained from lexi_drift_create.\n *      probs    : Array of probabilities corresponding to histogram bins.\n *                 Length must equal cfg->num_bins provided at construction.\n *      err      : Optional out-parameter for error status.\n *\n *  Notes\n *  -----\n *      Users are expected to pre-bucketize raw feature values into the same\n *      bin boundaries as the reference distribution used during model\n *      training.  All values in `probs` must be non-negative and sum to 1.0.\n */\nvoid\nlexi_drift_update(lexi_drift_detector_t* detector,\n                  const double*          probs,\n                  lexi_error_t*          err);\n\n/*\n *  Query whether drift has already been observed (non-destructive).\n *\n *  Returns\n *  -------\n *      true  : Drift condition currently active.\n *      false : No drift identified.\n */\nbool\nlexi_drift_is_drifting(const lexi_drift_detector_t* detector,\n                       double*                      out_score /* optional */);\n\n/*\n *  Attach an Observer callback.\n *\n *  The callback is invoked asynchronously *within the context of\n *  lexi_drift_update()* immediately after drift is detected. To prevent\n *  deadlocks, callbacks must not call back into the detector API.\n */\nlexi_error_t\nlexi_drift_add_listener(lexi_drift_detector_t* detector,\n                        lexi_drift_listener_t  fn,\n                        void*                  user_ctx);\n\n/*\n *  Remove an Observer callback.  All instances of `fn` with the same\n *  `user_ctx` will be removed.\n */\nlexi_error_t\nlexi_drift_remove_listener(lexi_drift_detector_t* detector,\n                           lexi_drift_listener_t  fn,\n                           void*                  user_ctx);\n\n#ifdef __cplusplus\n} /* extern \"C\" */\n#endif\n\n/* ====  Implementation  ===================================================== */\n#ifdef LEXILEARN_DRIFT_DETECTOR_IMPLEMENTATION\n/*  Internal helper macros  */\n#define LEXI_MIN(a,b) ((a) < (b) ? (a) : (b))\n#define LEXI_MAX(a,b) ((a) > (b) ? (a) : (b))\n\nstruct lexi_drift_detector\n{\n    lexi_drift_cfg_t    cfg;\n    size_t              sample_count;                  /* # observations      */\n    double              reference[LEXI_MAX_BINS];      /* Training dist.      */\n    double              rolling_actual[LEXI_MAX_BINS]; /* Sliding window dist */\n    double              last_score;\n    bool                drifting;\n\n    /* Observer Pattern */\n    lexi_drift_listener_t listeners[LEXI_MAX_LISTENERS];\n    void*                 listener_ctx[LEXI_MAX_LISTENERS];\n    size_t                listener_cnt;\n\n    /* Thread-safety */\n    pthread_mutex_t      mtx;\n};\n\n/* ====  Utility: Safe allocation wrapper  ================================== */\nstatic inline void* lexi_xcalloc(size_t n, size_t sz)\n{\n    void* p = calloc(n, sz);\n    return p;\n}\n\n/* ====  Metric Implementations  =========================================== */\nstatic double\nlexi_compute_psi(const double* ref, const double* act, size_t k)\n{\n    double psi = 0.0;\n    for (size_t i = 0; i < k; ++i)\n    {\n        const double e = ref[i] <= 0.0 ? 1e-12 : ref[i];\n        const double a = act[i] <= 0.0 ? 1e-12 : act[i];\n        psi += (a - e) * log(a / e);\n    }\n    return psi;\n}\n\nstatic double\nlexi_compute_kl(const double* ref, const double* act, size_t k)\n{\n    double kl = 0.0;\n    for (size_t i = 0; i < k; ++i)\n    {\n        double a = act[i] <= 0.0 ? 1e-12 : act[i];\n        double r = ref[i] <= 0.0 ? 1e-12 : ref[i];\n        kl += a * log(a / r);\n    }\n    return kl;\n}\n\nstatic double\nlexi_compute_wasserstein(const double* ref, const double* act, size_t k)\n{\n    /* 1-dimensional 1-Wasserstein distance for histograms */\n    double cum_ref = 0.0, cum_act = 0.0, wass = 0.0;\n    for (size_t i = 0; i < k; ++i)\n    {\n        cum_ref += ref[i];\n        cum_act += act[i];\n        wass += fabs(cum_ref - cum_act);\n    }\n    return wass;\n}\n\n/* ====  Private helper: notify listeners  ================================== */\nstatic void\nlexi_notify(const lexi_drift_detector_t* det)\n{\n    lexi_drift_event_t evt;\n    strncpy(evt.model_id, det->cfg.model_id, LEXI_MODEL_ID_LEN);\n    evt.score     = det->last_score;\n    evt.threshold = det->cfg.threshold;\n    evt.timestamp = time(NULL);\n\n    for (size_t i = 0; i < det->listener_cnt; ++i)\n    {\n        det->listeners[i](&evt, det->listener_ctx[i]);\n    }\n}\n\n/* ====  Public API: Create  ================================================= */\nlexi_drift_detector_t*\nlexi_drift_create(const lexi_drift_cfg_t* cfg, lexi_error_t* err)\n{\n    if (!cfg || cfg->num_bins == 0 || cfg->num_bins > LEXI_MAX_BINS)\n    {\n        if (err) *err = LEXI_EINVAL;\n        return NULL;\n    }\n\n    lexi_drift_detector_t* det = (lexi_drift_detector_t*)lexi_xcalloc(1, sizeof(*det));\n    if (!det)\n    {\n        if (err) *err = LEXI_ENOMEM;\n        return NULL;\n    }\n\n    det->cfg = *cfg;\n    /* Initialize reference distribution to uniform until calibrated */\n    for (size_t i = 0; i < cfg->num_bins; ++i)\n        det->reference[i] = 1.0 / (double)cfg->num_bins;\n\n    if (pthread_mutex_init(&det->mtx, NULL) != 0)\n    {\n        free(det);\n        if (err) *err = LEXI_ETHREAD;\n        return NULL;\n    }\n    if (err) *err = LEXI_OK;\n    return det;\n}\n\n/* ====  Public API: Destroy  ============================================== */\nvoid\nlexi_drift_destroy(lexi_drift_detector_t* det)\n{\n    if (!det) return;\n    pthread_mutex_destroy(&det->mtx);\n    free(det);\n}\n\n/* ====  Public API: Update  =============================================== */\nvoid\nlexi_drift_update(lexi_drift_detector_t* det,\n                  const double*          probs,\n                  lexi_error_t*          err)\n{\n    if (!det || !probs)\n    {\n        if (err) *err = LEXI_EINVAL;\n        return;\n    }\n\n    pthread_mutex_lock(&det->mtx);\n    const size_t k = det->cfg.num_bins;\n\n    /* Exponential moving average for rolling distribution */\n    const double alpha = 1.0 / (double)LEXI_MAX(1, det->cfg.window);\n    for (size_t i = 0; i < k; ++i)\n    {\n        double p = probs[i];\n        if (p < 0.0)\n        {\n            pthread_mutex_unlock(&det->mtx);\n            if (err) *err = LEXI_EINVAL;\n            return;\n        }\n        det->rolling_actual[i] =\n            (1.0 - alpha) * det->rolling_actual[i] + alpha * p;\n    }\n\n    /* Compute drift metric */\n    switch (det->cfg.metric)\n    {\n        case LEXI_DRIFT_PSI:\n            det->last_score = lexi_compute_psi(det->reference,\n                                               det->rolling_actual, k);\n            break;\n        case LEXI_DRIFT_KL:\n            det->last_score = lexi_compute_kl(det->reference,\n                                              det->rolling_actual, k);\n            break;\n        case LEXI_DRIFT_WASSER:\n            det->last_score = lexi_compute_wasserstein(det->reference,\n                                                       det->rolling_actual, k);\n            break;\n        default:\n            det->last_score = 0.0;\n            break;\n    }\n\n    bool drift_now = det->last_score >= det->cfg.threshold;\n    if (drift_now && !det->drifting)\n    {\n        det->drifting = true;\n        lexi_notify(det); /* fire Observer callbacks */\n    }\n    else if (!drift_now && det->drifting)\n    {\n        det->drifting = false; /* reset flag */\n    }\n\n    det->sample_count++;\n    pthread_mutex_unlock(&det->mtx);\n\n    if (err) *err = LEXI_OK;\n}\n\n/* ====  Public API: is_drifting  ========================================== */\nbool\nlexi_drift_is_drifting(const lexi_drift_detector_t* det, double* out_score)\n{\n    if (!det) return false;\n    if (out_score) *out_score = det->last_score;\n    return det->drifting;\n}\n\n/* ====  Public API: add/remove listener  =================================== */\nlexi_error_t\nlexi_drift_add_listener(lexi_drift_detector_t* det,\n                        lexi_drift_listener_t  fn,\n                        void*                  ctx)\n{\n    if (!det || !fn) return LEXI_EINVAL;\n    pthread_mutex_lock(&det->mtx);\n\n    if (det->listener_cnt >= LEXI_MAX_LISTENERS)\n    {\n        pthread_mutex_unlock(&det->mtx);\n        return LEXI_ELISTENER_FULL;\n    }\n    det->listeners[det->listener_cnt]     = fn;\n    det->listener_ctx[det->listener_cnt]  = ctx;\n    det->listener_cnt++;\n\n    pthread_mutex_unlock(&det->mtx);\n    return LEXI_OK;\n}\n\nlexi_error_t\nlexi_drift_remove_listener(lexi_drift_detector_t* det,\n                           lexi_drift_listener_t  fn,\n                           void*                  ctx)\n{\n    if (!det || !fn) return LEXI_EINVAL;\n\n    pthread_mutex_lock(&det->mtx);\n    size_t i = 0;\n    while (i < det->listener_cnt)\n    {\n        if (det->listeners[i] == fn && det->listener_ctx[i] == ctx)\n        {\n            /* shift elements */\n            for (size_t j = i + 1; j < det->listener_cnt; ++j)\n            {\n                det->listeners[j - 1]    = det->listeners[j];\n                det->listener_ctx[j - 1] = det->listener_ctx[j];\n            }\n            det->listener_cnt--;\n            /* do not increment i to catch duplicate matches */\n        }\n        else\n        {\n            ++i;\n        }\n    }\n    pthread_mutex_unlock(&det->mtx);\n    return LEXI_OK;\n}\n\n#endif /* LEXILEARN_DRIFT_DETECTOR_IMPLEMENTATION */\n#endif /* LEXILEARN_DRIFT_DETECTOR_H */\n",

Monitoring.\n *  -----------------------------------------------------------------\n *  The Model Monitor is responsible for:\n *    \u2022 Persistently tracking model-level metrics (latency, accuracy, drift, etc.)\n *    \u2022 Emitting Observer-pattern events to trigger automated retraining\n *    \u2022 Acting as an abstraction layer so that multiple drift-detection\n *      strategies can be swapped in without touching higher-level code\n *    \u2022 Interfacing with the Model Registry to tag / version promoted models\n *\n *  This header intentionally contains no implementation logic\u2014only the public\n *  contracts meant to be consumed by the Controller\u2019s Pipeline components\n *  and, where relevant, by View-layer dashboards.\n */\n\n#ifndef LEXILEARN_CONTROLLER_MONITORING_MODEL_MONITOR_H\n#define LEXILEARN_CONTROLLER_MONITORING_MODEL_MONITOR_H\n\n/* --- Standard Library ---------------------------------------------------- */\n#include <stdint.h>\n#include <stdbool.h>\n#include <stddef.h>\n#include <time.h>\n\n#ifdef __cplusplus\nextern \"C\" {\n#endif\n\n/* ------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n/*                               Versioning                                  */\n/* ------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n\n#define MODEL_MONITOR_VERSION_MAJOR  1\n#define MODEL_MONITOR_VERSION_MINOR  0\n#define MODEL_MONITOR_VERSION_PATCH  0\n\n/* ------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n/*                               Error Codes                                 */\n/* ------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n\ntypedef enum {\n    MM_OK = 0,                  /* Success */\n    MM_ERR_INVALID_ARG = -1,    /* Invalid function argument */\n    MM_ERR_MEM_ALLOC   = -2,    /* Memory allocation failure */\n    MM_ERR_IO          = -3,    /* ------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n/*                           Model Metrics & Tags                            */\n/* ------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n\n/* High-level KPI buckets. Extend as needed. */\ntypedef struct {\n    double accuracy;              /* Macro accuracy or other figure of merit */\n    double f1_score;              /* Weighted F1 */\n    double precision;\n    double recall;\n\n    double latency_ms;            /* Avg/95th-percentile inference latency */\n    double throughput_qps;        /* Queries per second */\n\n    double data_drift;            /* e.g., Population-stability index (PSI) */\n    double concept_drift;         /* e.g., Sudden change detection score */\n\n    time_t snapshot_time_utc;     /* When metrics were observed */\n} mm_metrics_t;\n\n/* Opaque handle to a registered model instance */\ntypedef struct mm_model_handle_s mm_model_handle_t;\n\n/* Enum of Observer events emitted by the monitor */\ntypedef enum {\n    MM_EVENT_METRIC_UPDATE,       /* Triggered whenever metrics are updated */\n    MM_EVENT_DRIFT_DETECTED,      /* Data or concept drift threshold crossed */\n    MM_EVENT_RETRAIN_TRIGGERED,   /* Automated retrain job has been scheduled */\n    MM_EVENT_ERROR                /* A non-recoverable error has occurred */\n} mm_event_type_t;\n\ntypedef struct {\n    mm_event_type_t type;\n    mm_status_t     status;       /* Relevant for MM_EVENT_ERROR */\n    mm_metrics_t    latest_metrics;\n    const char     *msg;          /* Human-readable, may be NULL */\n} mm_event_t;\n\n/* Observer callback signature */\ntypedef void (*mm_observer_fn)(const mm_event_t *event, void *user_data);\n\n/* ------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n/*                       Strategy: Drift-Detector API                        */\n/* ------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n\n/*\n * Implementations must adhere to this interface and register themselves\n * via mm_register_drift_detector(). See docs/DriftDetectorPlugin.md\n */\n\ntypedef struct {\n    /* Initialize detector for a specific model and baseline metrics. */\n    mm_status_t (*init)(mm_model_handle_t   *model,\n                        const mm_metrics_t  *baseline);\n\n    /* Feed real-time metrics into the detector. */\n    mm_status_t (*update)(const mm_metrics_t *current_metrics,\n                          bool               *drift_detected);\n\n    /* Optional: return a human-readable diagnostic message. */\n    const char *(*diagnostics)(void);\n\n    /* Clean up any resources. */\n    void (*destroy)(void);\n} mm_drift_detector_vtbl_t;\n\n/* ------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n/*                              Public  API                                  */\n/* ------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n\n/**\n * mm_init()\n * ----------------------------------------------------------------------\n * Global initialization that must be invoked once during Controller start-up.\n * @return MM_OK or error code\n */\nmm_status_t mm_init(void);\n\n/**\n * mm_shutdown()\n * ----------------------------------------------------------------------\n * Flush all outstanding metrics, close persistent stores, and free memory.\n */\nvoid mm_shutdown(void);\n\n/**\n * mm_model_register()\n * ----------------------------------------------------------------------\n * Register a model instance with the monitor. A handle is returned on\n * success and must be released with mm_model_unregister().\n *\n * @param model_id        Unique identifier from Model Registry, NUL-terminated\n * @param baseline        Baseline metrics collected during validation\n * @param handle_out      Output: opaque model handle\n * @return                MM_OK or error code\n */\nmm_status_t mm_model_register(const char        *model_id,\n                              const mm_metrics_t *baseline,\n                              mm_model_handle_t **handle_out);\n\n/**\n * mm_model_unregister()\n * ----------------------------------------------------------------------\n * Releases internal resources associated with a model handle.\n */\nmm_status_t mm_model_unregister(mm_model_handle_t *handle);\n\n/**\n * mm_submit_metrics()\n * ----------------------------------------------------------------------\n * Ingest runtime metrics for a given model. May be invoked from multiple\n * threads (internally synchronized).\n *\n * @param handle          Model handle obtained from mm_model_register()\n * @param metrics         Metrics snapshot\n * @return                MM_OK or error code\n */\nmm_status_t mm_submit_metrics(mm_model_handle_t *handle,\n                              const mm_metrics_t *metrics);\n\n/**\n * mm_add_observer()\n * ----------------------------------------------------------------------\n * Register an observer that listens for MM_EVENT_* events. Thread-safe.\n *\n * @param handle          Model handle (or NULL to subscribe globally)\n * @param fn              Callback function\n * @param user_data       Opaque pointer passed back to observer\n * @return                MM_OK or error code\n */\nmm_status_t mm_add_observer(mm_model_handle_t *handle,\n                            mm_observer_fn     fn,\n                            void              *user_data);\n\n/**\n * mm_remove_observer()\n *\n * Removes a previously registered observer. Safe to call from within the\n * callback itself (will take effect after callback returns).\n */\nmm_status_t mm_remove_observer(mm_model_handle_t *handle,\n                               mm_observer_fn     fn,\n                               void              *user_data);\n\n/**\n * mm_register_drift_detector()\n * ----------------------------------------------------------------------\n * Plug-in a new drift detection strategy. The detector becomes available\n * system-wide; individual models can opt in via configuration.\n *\n * @param name            Unique plugin name (e.g., \"PSI\", \"KS-Test\")\n * @param vtbl            Function table implementing the detector\n * @return                MM_OK or error code\n */\nmm_status_t mm_register_drift_detector(const char               *name,\n                                       const mm_drift_detector_vtbl_t *vtbl);\n\n/**\n * mm_force_retrain()\n * ----------------------------------------------------------------------\n * Imperative API to bypass thresholds and force a retrain cycle.\n * Mainly useful for A/B testing or hot-fix releases.\n */\nmm_status_t mm_force_retrain(mm_model_handle_t *handle,\n                             const char        *reason);\n\n/* ------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n/*                               Utilities                                   */\n/* ------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n\n/* Convenience macro to embed current source location in diagnostic logs. */\n#define MM_SRC_LOC  __FILE__, __LINE__, __func__\n\n#ifdef __cplusplus\n} /* extern \"C\" */\n#endif\n\n#endif /* LEXILEARN_CONTROLLER_MONITORING_MODEL_MONITOR_H */\n```",
